<script type="text/javascript">
    
    var RelativeUrl = function (url) {
        var text = '';
        if (url) text = url;
        return 'https://shop.supervalu.ie/shopping/' + text;
    };

    function onProductImageError(image) {
        var imageUrl = image.src,
            imagePath = imageUrl.substring(0, imageUrl.lastIndexOf('/') + 1),
            missingImageUrl = imagePath + 'missing-image.png';

        if (image.src !== missingImageUrl) {
            image.src = missingImageUrl;
        }
    }

</script>
